***залежь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залежь.html>за́лежь</a> (28234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залежь.html>за́лежь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">záležʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залежь.html>за́лежи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залежь.html>за́лежи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залежь.html>за́лежей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deposit, accumulation</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лежь</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лежь-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li>to meddle</li></ol>

***залепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ть</a> (14297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">залепля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to close up <i>(with)</i>, to stick up <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залепленный.html>зале́пленные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фара.html>фа́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zaléplennyje grjázʹju fáry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mud-stained headlights</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to glue up <i>(with)</i>, to paste up, to paste over <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, to deal/mete out <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчину</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zalepítʹ</b> komú-libo poščóčinu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give smb a slap in the face</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zalepítʹ</b> komú-libo dvójku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give smb a poor mark/grade</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьмы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>zalepíli</b> pjatʹ let tjurʹmy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was sent up for five years</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — залеплять, залепливать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-леп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залетать.html>залета́ть</a> (19260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залетать.html>залета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(in, into)</i></li>
<li>to fly <i>(as high as)</i>, to go up <i>(as far as)</i>, to fly <i>(as far as)</i>, to fly <i>(behind, beyond)</i></li>
<li>to land <i>(somewhere)</i> on the way, to make a stopover <i>(somewhere)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get into a fix, to get into a mess, to get something one doesn't want <i>(i.e. contract a sexually transmitted disease or become pregnant)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залетать.html>залета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to fly</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́ть</a> (12382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залетать.html>залета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(in, into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">múxa <b>zaletéla</b> v kómnatu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a fly flew into the room</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fly <i>(as high as)</i>, to go up <i>(as far as)</i>, to fly <i>(as far as)</i>, to fly <i>(behind, beyond)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">самолёт <b><a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:северный.html>Северный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полярный.html>поля́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">samoljót <b>zaletél</b> za Severnyj poljárnyj krug</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the aircraft crossed the Arctic circle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ограда.html>огра́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjač <b>zaletél</b> za ográdu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the ball flew over the fence</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to land <i>(somewhere)</i> on the way, to make a stopover <i>(somewhere)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get into a fix, to get into a mess, to get something one doesn't want <i>(i.e. contract a sexually transmitted disease or become pregnant)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:залететь.html>залете́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мене</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaletétʹ</b> na ekzámene</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fail an exam</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залечь.html>зале́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaléčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залегать.html>залега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie (down)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:залечь.html>зале́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaléčʹ</b> spatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">go off to bed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:залечь.html>зале́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берлога.html>берло́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaléčʹ</b> v berlógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take to its lair/den</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залечь.html>зале́чь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дно.html>дно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zaléčʹ na dno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lie low; keep a low profile</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lie in hiding [in wait]</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop flat</li></ol>

***залив.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́в</a> (5772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the vb. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour, shed, cast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from PIE <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂leybʰ-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lībō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I sprinkle, spill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀλείφω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aleíphō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to anoint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залив.html>зали́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залив.html>зали́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залив.html>зали́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gulf
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:персидский.html>перси́дский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Persídskij zalív</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The Persian Gulf</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bay</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short past adverbial perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заливать.html>залива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flood <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of bodies of water</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to fill up (with liquid)</li>
<li>to pour on, to spill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie, tell lies</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заливаться.html>залива́ться</a> (9791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заливаться.html>залива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залиться.html>зали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sink underwater</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заливать.html>залива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zalivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заливаться.html>залива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залиться.html>зали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to laugh loudly</li></ol>

***заливной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заливной.html>заливно́й</a> (22240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">залив-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaliv-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заливной.html>заливно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalivnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>floodable; flooded</li>
<li>used for filling
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заливной.html>заливна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zalivnája</b> trubá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">filling pipe</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jellied; cooked in jelly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заливной.html>заливна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zalivnája</b> rýba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">jellied fish</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> phonetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sonorous</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li>to pour on, to spill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to upload</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>?

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залиться.html>зали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заливаться.html>залива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to laugh loudly</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́г</a> (9387)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">založítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalóg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pawning, pawn</li>
<li>pledge, deposit, security</li>
<li>collateral</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">διάθεσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diáthesis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalóg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> voice <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a particular mode of inflecting or conjugating verbs, or a particular form of a verb</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalóg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> virgin land <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">land that has never been plowed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> abandoned land</li></ol>

***заложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a> (3007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">založítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закладывать.html>закла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to lay, to place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страница.html>страни́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>založítʹ</b> stranícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mark a page, to put in a bookmark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воротник.html>воротни́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>založítʹ</b> za vorotník</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put away a lot of booze</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lay the foundation <i>(of)</i>, to lay</li>
<li>to heap <i>(with)</i>, to pile <i>(with)</i>, to block up <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to pawn, to pledge, to mortgage</li>
<li>to harness, to put a horse, to get ready a carriage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to betray, to give up <i>(to police)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заложник.html>зало́жник</a> (8618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">založítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́г</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zalóg</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pledge, deposit, security</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложник.html>зало́жник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalóžnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложник.html>зало́жника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложник.html>зало́жники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложник.html>зало́жников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зало́жница</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зало́жнический</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hostage</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>ло́ж</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лож-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ник</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Salve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">salve</i>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залп.html>залп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zalp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залп.html>за́лпа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залп.html>за́лпы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залп.html>за́лпов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>salvo, volley
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залп.html>за́лпом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zálpom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in one sitting; in one gulp; at a stretch; blurting out</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
